 ayushmann-parineeti sang 'meri Pyaari Bindu', watch the video

 - kai saare moments hai jo aapako baandhe rakhte hai jaise boyfriend-garlfriend, maa-baap or bacchon kaa trek, college or room mets kii kahani aadi
 - The songs are threaded very well in the film
 haareyaa, ye javaani jaise gane screen par or bhi achche lagate hai

 film main kishor kumaar, rafi sahab, lata mangeshkar, aar di burman ke gaanon ko bhi behtareen tareeke se film kaa hissaa banaaya gaya he
 - Parineeti Chopra and Ayushmann Khurrana have done very good and natural acting which does not look forced
 vahiin baaki sah kalakaaron kii casting bhi behtareen he
 - The film has many interesting moments like eggplant recipe, Big Boss elimination, TV antennas, audio cassettes, missed calls of telephone
 - loketions, cinemetography, camera work bahut badhiya he
 The writing and one liners of the film are excellent
 kamjor kadiyaan- film main flashbek kii kahani or pregent story kai baar seens ko mix kar detii he
 It can be made a little easier
 - film main kahani kai jagahon par travel karti he jo shaayad strimaline kii jaati to aasaani se sabko samaj aa sakati thi

 climex kaaphi khinchaa-khinchaa he jise crisp kiya ja saktaa tha

 film ke digital or satellite ritis pehle hi bik chuke hai

 virus:haversahar seconds nae virus bana kar internet ke jariye logon ke computer or mobile main bhejte hai

 2
 Malware: Malware means software that is not security verified and damages your computer and mobile

 How to avoid: To avoid these, you need to be very cautious before installing any software

 3
 ddos atake:'dinayal of sarvice atake' internet ke jariye kiya jane vaale sabase khatarnaak hamalaa he

 is atake ke jariye havers aapkaa data diarect chori nahin karte balki internet ke trephic ko badha kar kisi bhi website ko spam se bhar dete hai jisase us website ko kholane vaala vyakti kaa bhi data chori ho saktaa he
 How to avoid: Enable filtering in the router's firewall to avoid ddos attacks

 4
 fishing:fishing ek aisi takanic he jiske jariye havers aapke computer or mobile par mail, chat or powep aid ke jariye phek login pej bhejte hai jo bilkul original log in pej jaisaa dikhataa he

 isi tarah kaa ek maamla madhya pradesh main bhi hua tha

 kya koi ek samudaay kaa vyakti apane samudaay ke logon se apane dharm ke aadhaar par vot maang saktaa he? kya yah bhrasht aacharan kii shrenee main aata he? kya ek samudaay kaa vyakti duusare samudaay ke pratyaashee ke liye apane samudaay ke logon se vot maang saktaa he ? kya kisi dharm guru ke kisi duusare ke liye dharm ke naam par vot maangana bhrasht aacharan hoga or pratyaashee kaa chunaav radd kiya jaae? Actually, how many right and wrong ways are there in India during the elections to ask for votes on the basis of religion, caste community etc
 or by religious gurus to vote in the name of religion by supporting someone in the election? The Supreme Court is hearing this
 supreme court ne maamle kii pehali sunwaayee ke dauraan centre sarkaar ko philhal party banane se inkaar kar diya he

 isamen centre sarkaar ko party nahin banaaya ja saktaa

 Today is the 116th death anniversary of Swami Vivekananda
 narendra nath kaa janm 12 janvari 1863 ko kolkata main hua tha
 Who later became known as Swami Vivekananda
 vivekanand ke bare main kaha jaataa he ki vah khud bhukhe rahakar atithiyon ko khaanaa khilaate the or baahar thand main so jate the
 He was of sharp acumen since childhood
 kam umr main hi unhone veda or darshan shaastra kaa gyaan hasil kar liya tha
 At the same time, whenever Vivekananda is talked about, his speech in the religion parliament of Chicago in the year 1893 is definitely talked about
 126 saal pehle 11 sitambar 1983 ko jab swami vivekanand ne apane bhaashan kii shuruyaat 'mere america bhaaiyon or bahanon' kahkar kii thi jiske baad sabhaagaar kai minuton tak taaliyon kii gunj har taraf goonjati rahi
 Let us know the special features of that speech of Swami Vivekananda: - Sisters and brothers of America, my affectionate and emphatic welcome has filled my heart with immense joy and i thank you on behalf of the oldest saint tradition in the world
 main aapako sabhi dharmon kii janani kii taraf se dhanyavad detaa hum or sabhi jatiyon, sampradaayon ke lakhon, karodon hinduon kii taraf se aapkaa aabhaar vyakt karata hum
 These 10 things of Swami Vivekananda will make your future - My thanks are also to some speakers, who have told this forum that the idea of tolerance in the world has spread from the countries of the far east
 mujhe garv he ki main ek aise dharm se hum, jisane duniya ko sahansheeltaa or saarvbhaumik sweekruti kaa paath padhaayaa
 We not only believe in universal tolerance, but we accept all religions of the world as the truth
 - mujhe garv he ki main us desh se hum jisane sabhi dharmon or sabhi deshon ke sataae gaye logon ko apane yahaan sharan di
 i am proud that we have cherished in our heart the sacred memories of Israel in which their shrines were destroyed by the Roman invaders and then they took refuge in South India
 mujhe garv he ki main ek aise dharm se hum jisane parsi dharm ke logon ko sharan di or lagaataar ab bhi unki madad kar rahaa he
